      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L529" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="529"></td>
        <td id="LC529" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">		<span class="pl-c1">\draw</span>[-&gt;] (ch) -- (tr) node[midway, above] {<span class="pl-c1">\textsc</span>{compound}};</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L530" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="530"></td>
        <td id="LC530" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">		<span class="pl-c1">\draw</span>[-&gt;] (b) -- (tr) node[midway, above] {<span class="pl-c1">\textsc</span>{arg1}};</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L531" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="531"></td>
        <td id="LC531" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">		<span class="pl-c1">\draw</span>[-&gt;] (th) to[out=90, in=90, looseness=.4] node[midway, above, inner sep=1mm] {<span class="pl-c1">\textsc</span>{bv}} (tr);</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L532" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="532"></td>
        <td id="LC532" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">		<span class="pl-c1">\node</span>[anchor=north, inner sep=0pt] at (b.south) {<span class="pl-c1">\textsc</span>{top}};</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L533" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="533"></td>
        <td id="LC533" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	<span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{tikzpicture}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L534" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="534"></td>
        <td id="LC534" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	<span class="pl-c1">\vspace</span>*{2mm}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L535" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="535"></td>
        <td id="LC535" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	<span class="pl-c1">\caption</span>{</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L536" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="536"></td>
        <td id="LC536" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">		A <span class="pl-c1">\delphin</span><span class="pl-cce">\ </span>MRS Dependencies (DM) representation.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L537" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="537"></td>
        <td id="LC537" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">		This is a simplified version of MRS.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L538" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="538"></td>
        <td id="LC538" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">		Nodes are the tokens in the sentence (rather than abstract predicates),</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L539" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="539"></td>
        <td id="LC539" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">		and some scopal information is dropped.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L540" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="540"></td>
        <td id="LC540" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L541" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="541"></td>
        <td id="LC541" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{subfigure}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L542" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="542"></td>
        <td id="LC542" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\caption</span>{<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L543" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="543"></td>
        <td id="LC543" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	MRS-based dependency graphs for the sentence</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L544" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="544"></td>
        <td id="LC544" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	<span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{The cherry tree blossomed},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L545" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="545"></td>
        <td id="LC545" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	based on the MRS given in Figure~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:fig:mrs}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L546" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="546"></td>
        <td id="LC546" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L547" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="547"></td>
        <td id="LC547" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{cl:fig:dep}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L548" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="548"></td>
        <td id="LC548" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{figure}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L549" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="549"></td>
        <td id="LC549" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L550" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="550"></td>
        <td id="LC550" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In practical applications of HPSG grammars,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L551" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="551"></td>
        <td id="LC551" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the full derivation trees and the full feature structures are often unwieldy,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L552" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="552"></td>
        <td id="LC552" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">containing far more information than necessary for the task at hand.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L553" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="553"></td>
        <td id="LC553" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">It is therefore often desirable to extract a concise semantic representation.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L554" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="554"></td>
        <td id="LC554" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>TODO check the Semantics chapter once it&#39;s written</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L555" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="555"></td>
        <td id="LC555" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L556" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="556"></td>
        <td id="LC556" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In computational linguistics,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L557" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="557"></td>
        <td id="LC557" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">a popular approach to semantics is to represent the meaning of a sentence as a <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{dependency graph},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L558" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="558"></td>
        <td id="LC558" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">as this enables the use of graph-based algorithms.<span class="pl-c1">\footnote</span>{<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L559" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="559"></td>
        <td id="LC559" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	In this section, we are concerned with <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{semantic} dependencies.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L560" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="560"></td>
        <td id="LC560" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	For <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{syntactic} dependencies, see <span class="pl-c1">\crossrefchaptert</span>{dg}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L561" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="561"></td>
        <td id="LC561" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	Some practical applications of HPSG use syntactic dependencies</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L562" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="562"></td>
        <td id="LC562" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	(including many applications of the Alpino grammar, discussed in Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:other:alpino}).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L563" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="563"></td>
        <td id="LC563" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L564" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="564"></td>
        <td id="LC564" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Several types of dependency graph have been proposed</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L565" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="565"></td>
        <td id="LC565" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">based on Minimal Recursion Semantics <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>[MRS;][]{CFPS2005a},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L566" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="566"></td>
        <td id="LC566" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">with varying levels of simplification.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L567" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="567"></td>
        <td id="LC567" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{oepen2006eds} observe that if every predicate has a unique</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L568" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="568"></td>
        <td id="LC568" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{intrinsic argument}, an MRS can be converted to a variable-free semantic representation,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L569" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="569"></td>
        <td id="LC569" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">by replacing each reference to a variable with a reference to the corresponding predicate.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L570" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="570"></td>
        <td id="LC570" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">They present Elementary Dependency Structures (EDS),</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L571" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="571"></td>
        <td id="LC571" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">semantic graphs which maintain predicate-argument structure but discard some scope information.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L572" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="572"></td>
        <td id="LC572" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(For many applications, scope information is less important than predicate-argument structure.)</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L573" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="573"></td>
        <td id="LC573" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{copestake2009dmrs} builds on this idea</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L574" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="574"></td>
        <td id="LC574" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">to create a more expressive graph-based representation called</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L575" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="575"></td>
        <td id="LC575" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Dependency Minimal Recursion Semantics (DMRS),</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L576" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="576"></td>
        <td id="LC576" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">which is fully interconvertible with MRS.<span class="pl-c1">\footnote</span>{<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L577" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="577"></td>
        <td id="LC577" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	More precisely, for DMRS and MRS to be fully interconvertible,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L578" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="578"></td>
        <td id="LC578" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	every predicate (except for quantifiers) must have an intrinsic argument,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L579" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="579"></td>
        <td id="LC579" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	and every variable must be the intrinsic argument of exactly one predicate.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L580" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="580"></td>
        <td id="LC580" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">} This expressivity is achieved by adding annotations on the edges to</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L581" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="581"></td>
        <td id="LC581" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">indicate scope information.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L582" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="582"></td>
        <td id="LC582" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Finally, <span class="pl-c1">\delphin</span><span class="pl-cce">\ </span>MRS Dependencies <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>[DM;][]{ivanova2012dm}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L583" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="583"></td>
        <td id="LC583" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">express predicate-argument structure purely in terms of the surface tokens,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L584" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="584"></td>
        <td id="LC584" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">without introducing any abstract predicates.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L585" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="585"></td>
        <td id="LC585" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A comparison of MRS, DMRS, and DM is given in Figures <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:fig:mrs} and~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:fig:dep}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L586" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="586"></td>
        <td id="LC586" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The existence of such dependency graph formalisms,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L587" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="587"></td>
        <td id="LC587" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">as well as software packages to manipulate such graphs <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{copestake2016pydmrs},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L588" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="588"></td>
        <td id="LC588" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">has made it easier to use HPSG grammars in a number of practical tasks,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L589" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="589"></td>
        <td id="LC589" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">as we will discuss in Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:downstream}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L590" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="590"></td>
        <td id="LC590" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L591" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="591"></td>
        <td id="LC591" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L592" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="592"></td>
        <td id="LC592" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>% \subsection{A brief history of HPSG grammar engineering}</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L593" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="593"></td>

</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L597" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="597"></td>
        <td id="LC597" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>% % GE: no need to repeat what Flickinger et al. cover in their chapter</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L598" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="598"></td>
        <td id="LC598" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>% % but probably a good idea to contrast grammar engineering and linguistic theorizing</span></td>

        <td id="L600" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="600"></td>
        <td id="LC600" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>% % EMB 2018-12-21 Maybe everything we were going to put here is ending up</span></td>

        <td id="L602" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="602"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L603" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="603"></td>
        <td id="LC603" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>% Current platforms:</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L604" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="604"></td>
        <td id="LC604" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>%     \begin{itemize}</span></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L605" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="605"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L606" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="606"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L607" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="607"></td>

        <td id="L608" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="608"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L610" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="610"></td>

</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L611" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="611"></td>
        <td id="LC611" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\section</span>{Development of HPSG resources}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L612" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="612"></td>
        <td id="LC612" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{cl:resources}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L613" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="613"></td>
        <td id="LC613" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L614" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="614"></td>
        <td id="LC614" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In this section we describe various projects that have developed computational resources on the basis of or inspired by HPSG.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L615" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="615"></td>
        <td id="LC615" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">As we&#39;ll discuss in Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:deployment} below,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L616" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="616"></td>
        <td id="LC616" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">such resources can be used both in linguistic hypothesis testing as well as in various practical applications.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L617" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="617"></td>
        <td id="LC617" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The intended purpose of the resources influences the form that they take.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L618" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="618"></td>
        <td id="LC618" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The CoreGram Project (Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:coregram}) and Babel (Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:other:babel} primarily target linguistic hypothesis testing,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L619" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="619"></td>
        <td id="LC619" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the Alpino and Enju parsers (Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:other:alpino} and <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:other:enju}) primarily target practical applications,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L620" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="620"></td>
        <td id="LC620" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and the <span class="pl-c1">\delphin</span><span class="pl-cce">\ </span>Consortium (section <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:delphin}) attempts to balance these two goals.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L621" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="621"></td>
        <td id="LC621" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L622" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="622"></td>
        <td id="LC622" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L623" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="623"></td>
        <td id="LC623" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsection</span>{CoreGram}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L624" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="624"></td>
        <td id="LC624" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{cl:coregram}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L625" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="625"></td>
        <td id="LC625" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L626" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="626"></td>
        <td id="LC626" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The CoreGram<span class="pl-c1">\footnote</span>{</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L627" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="627"></td>
        <td id="LC627" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	<span class="pl-c1">\url</span>{https://hpsg.hu-berlin.de/Projects/CoreGram.html}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L628" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="628"></td>
        <td id="LC628" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">} Project</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L629" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="629"></td>
        <td id="LC629" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">aims to produce large-scale HPSG grammars,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L630" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="630"></td>
        <td id="LC630" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">which share a common `core&#39; grammar <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{MuellerCoreGram}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L631" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="631"></td>
        <td id="LC631" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> https://hpsg.hu-berlin.de/~stefan/Pub/coregram.pdf</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L632" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="632"></td>
        <td id="LC632" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> https://hpsg.hu-berlin.de/~stefan/Pub/coregram-brief.pdf</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L633" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="633"></td>
        <td id="LC633" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">At the time of writing, large grammars have been produced for</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L634" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="634"></td>
        <td id="LC634" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">German <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{MuellerLehrbuch1},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L635" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="635"></td>
        <td id="LC635" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Danish <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{MOeDanish-language},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L636" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="636"></td>
        <td id="LC636" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Persian <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{MG2010a},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L637" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="637"></td>
        <td id="LC637" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Maltese <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{MuellerMalteseSketch},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L638" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="638"></td>
        <td id="LC638" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and Mandarin <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{ML2013a}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L639" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="639"></td>
        <td id="LC639" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Smaller grammars are also available for English, Yiddish, Spanish, French, and Hindi.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L640" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="640"></td>
        <td id="LC640" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L641" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="641"></td>
        <td id="LC641" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">All grammars are implemented</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L642" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="642"></td>
        <td id="LC642" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">in the TRALE system <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{MPR2002a-u,Penn2004a-u},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L643" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="643"></td>
        <td id="LC643" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">which accommodates a wide range of technical devices proposed in the literature, including:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L644" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="644"></td>
        <td id="LC644" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">phonologically empty elements,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L645" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="645"></td>
        <td id="LC645" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">relational constraints,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L646" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="646"></td>
        <td id="LC646" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">implications with complex antecedents,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L647" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="647"></td>
        <td id="LC647" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">cyclic feature structures,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L648" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="648"></td>
        <td id="LC648" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and macros.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L649" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="649"></td>
        <td id="LC649" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">It also accomodates an expressive morphological component.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L650" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="650"></td>
        <td id="LC650" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{MelnikHandWritten} observes that,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L651" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="651"></td>
        <td id="LC651" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">compared to other platforms like the LKB (see Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:delphin} below),</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L652" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="652"></td>
        <td id="LC652" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">this allows grammar engineers to directly implement a wider range of theoretical proposals.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L653" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="653"></td>
        <td id="LC653" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L654" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="654"></td>
        <td id="LC654" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">An important part of CoreGram is the sharing of grammatical constraints across grammars.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L655" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="655"></td>
        <td id="LC655" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Some general constraints hold for all grammars,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L656" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="656"></td>
        <td id="LC656" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">while others hold for a subset of the grammars,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L657" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="657"></td>
        <td id="LC657" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and some only hold for a single grammar.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L658" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="658"></td>
        <td id="LC658" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{MuellerCoreGram} describes this as a</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L659" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="659"></td>
        <td id="LC659" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">``bottom-up approach with cheating&#39;&#39; (p.43)<span class="pl-cce">\,</span>---<span class="pl-cce">\,</span>the aim is</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L660" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="660"></td>
        <td id="LC660" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">to analyse each language on its own terms (hence ``bottom-up&#39;&#39;),</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L661" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="661"></td>
        <td id="LC661" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">but to re-use analyses from existing grammars if possible (hence ``with cheating&#39;&#39;).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L662" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="662"></td>
        <td id="LC662" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> on ``bottom-up&#39;&#39;, cite Haspelmath, Dryer, Croft?</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L663" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="663"></td>
        <td id="LC663" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> p43 of https://hpsg.hu-berlin.de/~stefan/Pub/coregram.pdf</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L664" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="664"></td>
        <td id="LC664" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The use of a core set of constraints is motivated not just for practical reasons,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L665" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="665"></td>
        <td id="LC665" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">but also for theoretical ones.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L666" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="666"></td>
        <td id="LC666" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">By developing multiple grammars in parallel,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L667" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="667"></td>
        <td id="LC667" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">analyses can be improved by cross-linguistic comparison.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L668" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="668"></td>
        <td id="LC668" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The constraints encoded in the core grammar</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L669" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="669"></td>
        <td id="LC669" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">can be seen as an hypothesis about the structure of human language.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L670" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="670"></td>
        <td id="LC670" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> GE 2019-02-25 aN hypothesis?</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L671" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="671"></td>
        <td id="LC671" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> I definitely don&#39;t say that, but I&#39;m happy to follow your spelling!</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L672" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="672"></td>
        <td id="LC672" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> We currently also have ``a history&#39;&#39; and ``a high-dimensional vector&#39;&#39; elsewhere</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L673" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="673"></td>
        <td id="LC673" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">as we will discuss in Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:lang-doc:coregram}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L674" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="674"></td>
        <td id="LC674" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L675" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="675"></td>
        <td id="LC675" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">CoreGram grammar development aims to incrementally increase coverage of each language.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L676" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="676"></td>
        <td id="LC676" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">To measure progress, grammars are evaluated against test suites,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L677" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="677"></td>
        <td id="LC677" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">collections of sentences each annotated with a grammaticality judgment <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{ONK97a,Mueller2004f}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L678" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="678"></td>
        <td id="LC678" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">This allows a grammarian to check for unexpected side effects when modifying a grammar,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L679" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="679"></td>
        <td id="LC679" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">to avoid situations when implementing an analysis of one phenomenon</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L680" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="680"></td>
        <td id="LC680" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">would break the analysis of another phenomenon.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L681" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="681"></td>
        <td id="LC681" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">This is particularly important when modifying a constraint that is used by several grammars.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L682" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="682"></td>
        <td id="LC682" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">To help achieve these aims, grammar development is supported by a range of software tools,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L683" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="683"></td>
        <td id="LC683" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">including the test suite tool <span class="pl-c1">\itsdb</span> (<span class="pl-c1">\citealp</span>{Oepen:01}; see also Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:delphin}),</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L684" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="684"></td>
        <td id="LC684" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and the graphical debugging tool Kahina <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{DER2010a-u,DER2013a}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L685" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="685"></td>
        <td id="LC685" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L686" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="686"></td>
        <td id="LC686" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L687" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="687"></td>
        <td id="LC687" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsection</span>{The <span class="pl-c1">\delphin</span><span class="pl-cce">\ </span>Consortium}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L688" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="688"></td>
        <td id="LC688" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{cl:delphin}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L689" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="689"></td>
        <td id="LC689" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L690" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="690"></td>
        <td id="LC690" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The <span class="pl-c1">\delphin\footnote</span>{This stands for DEep Linguistic</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L691" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="691"></td>
        <td id="LC691" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Processing in <span class="pl-c1">\textsc</span>{Hpsg} INitiative; see <span class="pl-c1">\url</span>{http://www.delph-in.net}} Consortium</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L692" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="692"></td>
        <td id="LC692" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">was established in 2001 to facilitate the development of large-scale,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L693" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="693"></td>
        <td id="LC693" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">linguistically motivated HPSG grammars for multiple languages in tandem</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L694" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="694"></td>
        <td id="LC694" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">with the software required for developing them and deploying them in</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L695" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="695"></td>
        <td id="LC695" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">practical applications. At the time that <span class="pl-c1">\delphin</span><span class="pl-cce">\ </span>was founded, the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L696" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="696"></td>
        <td id="LC696" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">English Resource Grammar</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L697" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="697"></td>
        <td id="LC697" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>[ERG;][]{Flickinger2000a,Flickinger2011a-u} had been under</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L698" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="698"></td>
        <td id="LC698" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">development already for 8 years and the Verbmobil project</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L699" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="699"></td>
        <td id="LC699" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{Wahlster2000a-ed} had also spurred the development of grammars for</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L700" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="700"></td>
        <td id="LC700" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">German <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>[GG;][]{MK2000a-cr,Crysmann2003b} and Japanese</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L701" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="701"></td>
        <td id="LC701" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>[Jacy;][]{SBB2016a}. Project DeepThought</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L702" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="702"></td>
        <td id="LC702" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{Callmeier-etal:2004} was exploring methodologies for combining</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L703" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="703"></td>

Supertagging helps some here, too, but other strategies include <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{sentence chunking}, or the task of breaking a long sentence into smaller ones without loss of meaning <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{muszynska:2016:ACL-SRW}.</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L785" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="785"></td>
        <td id="LC785" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Working with real-world text (rather than curated testsuites designed</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L786" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="786"></td>
        <td id="LC786" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">for linguistic research only) requires </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L787" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="787"></td>
        <td id="LC787" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the integration of external components such as morphological</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L788" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="788"></td>
        <td id="LC788" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">analyzers <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>[<span class="pl-c1">\eg</span>][]{Marimon2013a-u} and named entity recognizers <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>[<span class="pl-c1">\eg</span>][]{L06-1115,Sch:Usz:Fed:08}. As described in Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:prac:rank}, working with real-world applications requires parse ranking <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>[<span class="pl-c1">\eg</span>][]{Tou:Man:Fli:Oep:05}, and similarly ranking of generator outputs (known as <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{realization ranking}; <span class="pl-c1">\citealt</span>[<span class="pl-c1">\eg</span>][]{Velldal:09}). Finally, research on embedding broad-coverage grammars in practical applications inspires work  towards making sure that the semantic</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L789" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="789"></td>
        <td id="LC789" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">representations can serve as a suitable interface for external</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L790" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="790"></td>
        <td id="LC790" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">components <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>[<span class="pl-c1">\eg</span>][]{flickinger2005sem}. </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L791" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="791"></td>
        <td id="LC791" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> EMB 2018-12-21 I can probably put in citations for all of those</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L792" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="792"></td>

        <td id="L796" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="796"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L797" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="797"></td>
        <td id="LC797" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">These efforts are also valuable from a strictly linguistic point of view, <span class="pl-c1">\ie</span><span class="pl-cce">\ </span>one not concerned with practical applications.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L798" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="798"></td>
        <td id="LC798" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">First, the broader the coverage of a grammar,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L799" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="799"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>

        <td id="L808" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="808"></td>
        <td id="LC808" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L809" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="809"></td>
        <td id="LC809" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsubsection</span>{Alpino}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L810" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="810"></td>
        <td id="LC810" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{cl:other:alpino}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L811" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="811"></td>
        <td id="LC811" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L812" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="812"></td>
        <td id="LC812" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Alpino<span class="pl-c1">\footnote</span>{<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L813" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="813"></td>
        <td id="LC813" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	<span class="pl-c1">\url</span>{http://www.let.rug.nl/vannoord/alp/Alpino/}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L814" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="814"></td>
        <td id="LC814" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L815" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="815"></td>
        <td id="LC815" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">is a broad-coverage grammar of Dutch</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L816" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="816"></td>
        <td id="LC816" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{BvNM2001a-u,vannoord2005alpino,vannoord2006alpino}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L817" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="817"></td>
        <td id="LC817" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> https://www.let.rug.nl/vannoord/papers/alpino.pdf</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L818" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="818"></td>
        <td id="LC818" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> https://www.let.rug.nl/vannoord/papers/wcpsavg.pdf</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L819" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="819"></td>
        <td id="LC819" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> http://talnarchives.atala.org/TALN/TALN-2006/taln-2006-invite-002.pdf</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L820" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="820"></td>
        <td id="LC820" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The main motivation is practical: to provide coverage and accuracy</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L821" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="821"></td>
        <td id="LC821" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">comparable to state-of-the-art parsers for English.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L822" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="822"></td>
        <td id="LC822" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Nonetheless, it also includes theoretically interesting analyses,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L823" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="823"></td>
        <td id="LC823" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">such as for cross-serial dependencies <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{BvN98a}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L824" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="824"></td>
        <td id="LC824" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In addition to using hand-written rules,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L825" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="825"></td>
        <td id="LC825" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">lexical information (such as subcategorisation frames) has also been extracted from two existing lexicons,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L826" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="826"></td>
        <td id="LC826" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Celex <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{baayen1995celex}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L827" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="827"></td>
        <td id="LC827" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and Parole <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{kruyt1997parole}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L828" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="828"></td>
        <td id="LC828" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L829" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="829"></td>
        <td id="LC829" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Alpino produces syntactic dependency graphs,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L830" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="830"></td>
        <td id="LC830" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">following the annotation format of the Spoken Dutch Corpus <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{oostdijk2000corpus}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L831" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="831"></td>
        <td id="LC831" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">These dependencies are constructed directly in the feature-structure formalism,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L832" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="832"></td>
        <td id="LC832" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">exploiting the fact that a feature structure can be formalised as a directed acyclic graph.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L833" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="833"></td>
        <td id="LC833" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Each lexical entry encodes a partial dependency graph,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L834" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="834"></td>
        <td id="LC834" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and these graphs are composed through phrase structure rules</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L835" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="835"></td>
        <td id="LC835" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">to give a dependency graph for a whole sentence.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L836" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="836"></td>
        <td id="LC836" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L837" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="837"></td>
        <td id="LC837" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Although these dependencies differ from the semantic dependencies discussed in Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:prac:dep},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L838" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="838"></td>
        <td id="LC838" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">a common motivation is to make the representations easier to use in practical applications.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L839" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="839"></td>
        <td id="LC839" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">To harmonize with other computational work on dependency parsing,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L840" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="840"></td>
        <td id="LC840" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{Bou:Van:17} have also producing a mapping from this format</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L841" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="841"></td>
        <td id="LC841" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">to Universal Dependencies <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>[UD;][]{Niv:Mar:Gin:16},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L842" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="842"></td>
        <td id="LC842" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">as discussed in Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:lang-doc:treebanks} below.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L843" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="843"></td>
        <td id="LC843" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Alpino uses a statistical model trained on a dependency treebank,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L844" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="844"></td>
        <td id="LC844" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and in fact the same statistical model can be used in both parsing and generation <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{dekok2011reversible}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L845" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="845"></td>
        <td id="LC845" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L846" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="846"></td>
        <td id="LC846" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L847" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="847"></td>
        <td id="LC847" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsubsection</span>{Enju}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L848" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="848"></td>
        <td id="LC848" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{cl:other:enju}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L849" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="849"></td>
        <td id="LC849" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L850" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="850"></td>
        <td id="LC850" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Enju<span class="pl-c1">\footnote</span>{<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L851" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="851"></td>
        <td id="LC851" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	<span class="pl-c1">\url</span>{http://www.nactem.ac.uk/enju/}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L852" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="852"></td>
        <td id="LC852" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L853" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="853"></td>
        <td id="LC853" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">is a broad-coverage grammar of English,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L854" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="854"></td>
        <td id="LC854" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">semi-automatically acquired from the Penn Treebank <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{MNT2005a-u}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L855" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="855"></td>
        <td id="LC855" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">This approach aims to reduce the cost of writing a grammar</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L856" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="856"></td>
        <td id="LC856" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">by leveraging existing resources.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L857" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="857"></td>
        <td id="LC857" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The basic idea is that, by viewing Penn Treebank trees as partial specifications of HPSG derivations,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L858" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="858"></td>
        <td id="LC858" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">it is possible to infer lexical entries.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L859" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="859"></td>
        <td id="LC859" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L860" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="860"></td>
        <td id="LC860" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citeauthor</span>{MNT2005a-u} converted the relatively flat trees in the Penn Treebank to binary-branching trees,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L861" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="861"></td>
        <td id="LC861" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and percolated head information through the trees.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L862" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="862"></td>
        <td id="LC862" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">They also had to convert analyses for certain constructions,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L863" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="863"></td>
        <td id="LC863" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">including subject-control verbs, auxiliary verbs, coordination, and extracted arguments.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L864" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="864"></td>
        <td id="LC864" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Each converted tree can then be combined with a small set of hand-written HPSG schemata,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L865" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="865"></td>
        <td id="LC865" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">to induce a lexical entry for each word in the sentence.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L866" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="866"></td>
        <td id="LC866" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L867" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="867"></td>
        <td id="LC867" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Development of Enju has focused on performance in practical applications,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L868" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="868"></td>
        <td id="LC868" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and the grammar is supported by an efficient parser <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{tsuruoka2004enju,matsuzaki2007supertag},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L869" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="869"></td>
        <td id="LC869" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">using a probabilistic model for feature structures <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{MT2008a-u}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L870" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="870"></td>

</td>

        <td id="L909" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="909"></td>
        <td id="LC909" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">As decribed in <span class="pl-c1">\citealt</span>{Mueller99a-Short,Bender2008c-Short} and <span class="pl-c1">\citealt</span>{BFO2011a-u},</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC910" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">grammar engineering, that is the building of grammars in software, is</td>
      </tr>

      </tr>

      <tr>
        <td id="L933" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="933"></td>

      </tr>

</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L940" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="940"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="L941" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="941"></td>

      </tr>

      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L960" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="960"></td>
        <td id="LC960" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">development of <span class="pl-c1">\delphin</span>-style grammars for additional languages. It</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L961" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="961"></td>

      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>

      </tr>

</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1005" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1005"></td>

</td>
      </tr>

      </tr>

      <tr>
        <td id="L1014" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1014"></td>
        <td id="LC1014" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">AGGREGATION starts from two observations: (1) Descriptive linguists</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1015" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1015"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1016" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1016"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1017" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1017"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1018" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1018"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1019" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1019"></td>
        <td id="LC1019" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">high-level typological properties or specific constraints on lexical</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1020" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1020"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1021" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1021"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1022" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1022"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1023" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1023"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1024" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1024"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1025" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1025"></td>
        <td id="LC1025" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">linguistic subsystems. For example, it learns morphotactics by</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1026" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1026"></td>
        <td id="LC1026" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">observing morpheme order in the training data, and the grouping</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1027" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1027"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1028" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1028"></td>
        <td id="LC1028" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">stems they attach to <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{Wax:14,Zamaraeva:17}. For many kinds of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1029" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1029"></td>
        <td id="LC1029" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">syntactic information, it leverages syntactic structure projected from</td>
      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>

      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1034" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1034"></td>

      </tr>

TypeGram provides methods of creating HPSG grammars by encoding specifications of valence and inflection in particularly rich IGT and then creating grammars based on those specifications.}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1036" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1036"></td>

      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1038" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1038"></td>
        <td id="LC1038" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{cl:lang-doc:treebanks}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1039" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1039"></td>
        <td id="LC1039" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>Emily</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1040" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1040"></td>
        <td id="LC1040" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1041" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1041"></td>
        <td id="LC1041" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A particularly valuable type of resource that can be derived from HPSG</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1042" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1042"></td>
        <td id="LC1042" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">grammars are treebanks and sembanks. A treebank is a collection of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1043" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1043"></td>
        <td id="LC1043" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">text where each sentence is associated with a syntactic</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1044" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1044"></td>
        <td id="LC1044" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">representation. A sembank has semantic representations (in some cases</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1045" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1045"></td>
        <td id="LC1045" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">in addition to the syntactic ones). Treebanks and sembanks can be used</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1046" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1046"></td>
        <td id="LC1046" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">for linguistic research, as the analyses allow for more detailed</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1047" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1047"></td>
        <td id="LC1047" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">structure-based searches for phenomena of interest <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{Rohde:05,Gho:Bir:10,Kou:Oep:14}.<span class="pl-c1">\footnote</span>{The WeSearch interface of <span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{Kou:Oep:14} can be accessed at <span class="pl-c1">\url</span>{http://wesearch.delph-in.net/deepbank/search.jsp}}</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1054" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1054"></td>
