      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1055" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1055"></td>
        <td id="LC1055" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">treebanks can also be a valuable addition, helping readers connect</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1056" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1056"></td>
        <td id="LC1056" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">prose descriptions of linguistic phenomena to multiple examples in the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1057" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1057"></td>
        <td id="LC1057" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">corpus <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{Ben:Gho:Bal:Dri:12}. In natural language processing,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1058" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1058"></td>
        <td id="LC1058" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">treebanks and sembanks are critical source material for training</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1059" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1059"></td>
        <td id="LC1059" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">stochastic and neural parsers (see Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:downstream:data}).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1060" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1060"></td>
        <td id="LC1060" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1061" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1061"></td>
        <td id="LC1061" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Traditional treebanks are created by doing a certain amount of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1062" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1062"></td>
        <td id="LC1062" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">preprocessing on data, including possibly chunking or CFG parsing, and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1063" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1063"></td>
        <td id="LC1063" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">then hand-correcting the result <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{Mar:San:Mar:93,Ban:Bon:Cai:13}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1064" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1064"></td>
        <td id="LC1064" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">While this approach is a means to encode human insight about</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1065" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1065"></td>
        <td id="LC1065" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">linguistic structure for later automatic processing, it is both</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1066" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1066"></td>
        <td id="LC1066" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">inefficient and potentially error-prone. The Alpino project</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1067" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1067"></td>
        <td id="LC1067" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{vanderbeek2002alpino} addresses this by first parsing the text</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1068" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1068"></td>
        <td id="LC1068" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">with a broad-coverage HPSG-inspired grammar of Dutch and then having</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1069" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1069"></td>
        <td id="LC1069" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">annotators select among the parses. The selection process is</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1070" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1070"></td>
        <td id="LC1070" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">facilitated by allowing the annotators to mark potential lexical</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1071" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1071"></td>
        <td id="LC1071" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">entries for words in the sentence at hand as correct, possibly</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1072" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1072"></td>
        <td id="LC1072" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">correct, or wrong and to pre-mark some constituent boundaries. These</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1073" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1073"></td>
        <td id="LC1073" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">constraints reduce the search space for the parser and consequently</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1074" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1074"></td>
        <td id="LC1074" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">also the range of analyses the annotator has to consider before</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1075" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1075"></td>
        <td id="LC1075" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">choosing one. A facility for adding one-off lexical entries to handle</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1076" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1076"></td>
        <td id="LC1076" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\eg</span><span class="pl-cce">\ </span>misspellings helps increase grammar coverage.  Disambiguation is</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1077" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1077"></td>
        <td id="LC1077" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">handled with the aid of <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{discriminants} <span class="pl-c1">\ie</span><span class="pl-cce">\ </span>properties true of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1078" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1078"></td>
        <td id="LC1078" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">some but not all trees in the parse forest <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{Carter:97}. Finally,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1079" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1079"></td>
        <td id="LC1079" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the annotators may further edit analyses deemed insufficient. Though</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1080" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1080"></td>
        <td id="LC1080" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the underlying grammar is based on HPSG, the treebank stores</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1081" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1081"></td>
        <td id="LC1081" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">dependency representations instead.  The Alpino parser was similarly</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1082" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1082"></td>
        <td id="LC1082" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">used to construct the Lassy treebanks of written Dutch</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1083" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1083"></td>
        <td id="LC1083" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{van:bou:van:13}.  In more recent work, these dependency</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1084" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1084"></td>
        <td id="LC1084" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">representations have been mapped to the Universal Dependencies (UD)</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1085" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1085"></td>
        <td id="LC1085" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">annotation standards <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{Niv:Mar:Gin:16} to produce a UD treebank</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1086" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1086"></td>
        <td id="LC1086" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">for Dutch <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{Bou:Van:17}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1087" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1087"></td>
        <td id="LC1087" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1088" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1088"></td>
        <td id="LC1088" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The Redwoods project <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{OFTM2004a-u} also produces grammar-driven</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1089" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1089"></td>
        <td id="LC1089" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">treebanks, in this case for English and without any post-editing of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1090" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1090"></td>
        <td id="LC1090" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">analyses.<span class="pl-c1">\footnote</span>{There are also Redwoods-style treebanks for other</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1091" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1091"></td>
        <td id="LC1091" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  languages, including the Hinoki Treebank of Japanese</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1092" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1092"></td>
        <td id="LC1092" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{bond:etal:2004} and the Tibidabo Treebank of Spanish</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1093" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1093"></td>
        <td id="LC1093" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{marimon:2015}.}  As with Alpino, this is done by first</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1094" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1094"></td>
        <td id="LC1094" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">parsing the corpus with the grammar and calcuating the discriminants</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1095" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1095"></td>
        <td id="LC1095" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">for each parse forest.  Finally, the treebanking software stores not</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1096" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1096"></td>
        <td id="LC1096" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">only the final full HPSG analysis that was selected, but also the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1097" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1097"></td>
        <td id="LC1097" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">decisions the annotator made about each discriminant. Thus when the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1098" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1098"></td>
        <td id="LC1098" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">grammar is updated to include for example a refinement to the semantic</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1099" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1099"></td>
        <td id="LC1099" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">representations, the corpus can be reparsed and the decisions</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1100" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1100"></td>
        <td id="LC1100" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">replayed, leaving only a small amount of further annotation work to be</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1101" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1101"></td>
        <td id="LC1101" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">done to handle any additional ambguity introduced. The activity of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1102" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1102"></td>
        <td id="LC1102" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">treebanking in turn provides useful insight into grammatical analyses,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1103" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1103"></td>
        <td id="LC1103" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">including sources of spurious ambiguity and phenomena that are not yet</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1104" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1104"></td>
        <td id="LC1104" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">properly handled and thus informs and spurs further grammar</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1105" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1105"></td>
        <td id="LC1105" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">development.  A downside to strictly grammar-based treebanking is that</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1106" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1106"></td>
        <td id="LC1106" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">only items for which the grammar finds a reasonable parse can be</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1107" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1107"></td>
        <td id="LC1107" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">included in the treebank. For many applications, this is not a</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1108" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1108"></td>
        <td id="LC1108" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">drawback, so long as there are sufficient and sufficiently varied</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1109" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1109"></td>
        <td id="LC1109" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">sentences that do receive analyses.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1110" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1110"></td>
        <td id="LC1110" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1111" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1111"></td>
        <td id="LC1111" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Finally, there are also automatically annotated treebanks.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1112" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1112"></td>
        <td id="LC1112" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">These are not as reliable as manually annotated treebanks,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1113" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1113"></td>
        <td id="LC1113" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">but they can be considerably larger.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1114" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1114"></td>
        <td id="LC1114" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">WikiWoods<span class="pl-c1">\footnote</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\url</span>{http://moin.delph-in.net/WikiWoods}}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1115" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1115"></td>
        <td id="LC1115" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">covers 55m sentences of English (900m tokens).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1116" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1116"></td>
        <td id="LC1116" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">It was produced by <span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{flickinger2010wikiwoods} and <span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{solberg2012wikiwoods}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1117" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1117"></td>
        <td id="LC1117" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">from the July 2008 dump of the full English Wikipedia,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1118" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1118"></td>
        <td id="LC1118" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">using the ERG and PET,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1119" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1119"></td>
        <td id="LC1119" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">with parse ranking trained on the manually treebanked subcorpus WeScience <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{ytrestol2009wescience}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1120" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1120"></td>
        <td id="LC1120" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">As with the Redwoods treebanks, WikiWoods is updated with each release of the ERG.</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1121" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1121"></td>

      </tr>

</td>
      </tr>
