</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1124" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1124"></td>
        <td id="LC1124" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsection</span>{Downstream applications}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1125" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1125"></td>
        <td id="LC1125" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{cl:downstream}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1126" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1126"></td>
        <td id="LC1126" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>Guy</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1127" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1127"></td>
        <td id="LC1127" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1128" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1128"></td>
        <td id="LC1128" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In this section, we discuss</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1129" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1129"></td>
        <td id="LC1129" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the use of HPSG grammars for practical tasks.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1130" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1130"></td>
        <td id="LC1130" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">There is a large number of applications,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1131" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1131"></td>
        <td id="LC1131" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and we focus on several important applications here.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1132" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1132"></td>
        <td id="LC1132" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:downstream:edu},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1133" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1133"></td>
        <td id="LC1133" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">we cover educational applications where a grammar is used directly.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1134" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1134"></td>
        <td id="LC1134" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:downstream:nlp},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1135" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1135"></td>
        <td id="LC1135" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">we cover applications where a grammar is used to provide features</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1136" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1136"></td>
        <td id="LC1136" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">to help solve tasks in Natural Language Processing (NLP).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1137" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1137"></td>
        <td id="LC1137" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Finally, in Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:downstream:data},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1138" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1138"></td>
        <td id="LC1138" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">we cover applications where a grammar is used to provide data for machine learning systems.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1139" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1139"></td>
        <td id="LC1139" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Within the <span class="pl-c1">\delphin</span><span class="pl-cce">\ </span>community,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1140" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1140"></td>
        <td id="LC1140" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">a regularly updated list of applications is available online.<span class="pl-c1">\footnote</span>{<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1141" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1141"></td>
        <td id="LC1141" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	<span class="pl-c1">\url</span>{http://moin.delph-in.net/DelphinApplications}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1142" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1142"></td>
        <td id="LC1142" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1143" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1143"></td>
        <td id="LC1143" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1144" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1144"></td>
        <td id="LC1144" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1145" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1145"></td>
        <td id="LC1145" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsubsection</span>{Education}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1146" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1146"></td>
        <td id="LC1146" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{cl:downstream:edu}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1147" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1147"></td>
        <td id="LC1147" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1148" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1148"></td>
        <td id="LC1148" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Precise syntatic analyses can be useful in language teaching,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1149" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1149"></td>
        <td id="LC1149" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">in order to automatically identify errors and give feedback to the student.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1150" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1150"></td>
        <td id="LC1150" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In order to model common mistakes,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1151" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1151"></td>
        <td id="LC1151" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">a grammar can be extended with so-called ``mal-rules&#39;&#39;.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1152" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1152"></td>
        <td id="LC1152" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A mal-rule is like a normal rule, in that it licenses a construction,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1153" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1153"></td>
        <td id="LC1153" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and can be treated the same during parsing<span class="pl-cce">\,</span>---<span class="pl-cce">\,</span>however, given a parse,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1154" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1154"></td>
        <td id="LC1154" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the presence of mal-rules indicates that the student needs to be given feedback</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1155" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1155"></td>
        <td id="LC1155" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{Ben:Fli:Oep:04,flickinger2013error,morgadodacosta2016error}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1156" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1156"></td>
        <td id="LC1156" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A large scale system implementing this kind of computer-aided teaching has been developed</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1157" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1157"></td>
        <td id="LC1157" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">by the Education Program for Gifted Youth at Stanford University,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1158" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1158"></td>
        <td id="LC1158" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">using the ERG <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{suppes2014teach}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1159" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1159"></td>
        <td id="LC1159" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">This system has reached tens of thousands of elementary and middle school children,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1160" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1160"></td>
        <td id="LC1160" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and has been found to improve the school results of underachieving children.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1161" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1161"></td>
        <td id="LC1161" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> Redbird (McGraw-Hill)</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1162" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1162"></td>
        <td id="LC1162" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1163" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1163"></td>
        <td id="LC1163" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Another way to use a precision grammar is to automatically produce teaching materials.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1164" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1164"></td>
        <td id="LC1164" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Given a semantic representation,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1165" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1165"></td>
        <td id="LC1165" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">a grammar can generate one or more sentences.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1166" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1166"></td>
        <td id="LC1166" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{Flickinger:17} uses the ERG to produce practice exercises for a student learning first-order logic.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1167" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1167"></td>
        <td id="LC1167" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For each exercise, the student is presented with a natural language sentence</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1168" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1168"></td>
        <td id="LC1168" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and is supposed to write down the corresponding first-order logical form.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1169" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1169"></td>
        <td id="LC1169" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">By using a grammar, the system can produce syntactically varied questions</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1170" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1170"></td>
        <td id="LC1170" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and automatically evaluate the student&#39;s answer.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1171" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1171"></td>
        <td id="LC1171" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1172" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1172"></td>
        <td id="LC1172" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1173" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1173"></td>
        <td id="LC1173" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsubsection</span>{NLP tasks}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1174" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1174"></td>
        <td id="LC1174" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{cl:downstream:nlp}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1175" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1175"></td>
        <td id="LC1175" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1176" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1176"></td>
        <td id="LC1176" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Much NLP work focuses on specific <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{tasks},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1177" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1177"></td>
        <td id="LC1177" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where a system is presented with some input,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1178" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1178"></td>
        <td id="LC1178" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and required to produce an output,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1179" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1179"></td>
        <td id="LC1179" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">with a clearly-defined metric to determine how well the system performs.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1180" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1180"></td>
        <td id="LC1180" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">HPSG grammars have been used in a range of such tasks,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1181" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1181"></td>
        <td id="LC1181" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where the syntactic and semantic analyses provide useful features.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1182" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1182"></td>
        <td id="LC1182" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1183" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1183"></td>
        <td id="LC1183" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{Information retrieval} is the task of finding relevant documents for a given query.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1184" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1184"></td>
        <td id="LC1184" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For example, <span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{schaefer2011acl} present a tool for searching the ACL Anthology, using the ERG.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1185" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1185"></td>
        <td id="LC1185" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{Information extraction} is the task of identifying useful facts in a collection of documents.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1186" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1186"></td>
        <td id="LC1186" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For example, <span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{reiplinger2012glossary} aim to identify definitions of technical concepts,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1187" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1187"></td>
        <td id="LC1187" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">in order to automatically construct a glossary.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1188" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1188"></td>
        <td id="LC1188" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">They find that using the ERG reduces noise in the candidate definitions.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1189" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1189"></td>
        <td id="LC1189" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{miyao2008protein} aim to identify protein-protein interactions in the biomedical literature, using Enju.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1190" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1190"></td>
        <td id="LC1190" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1191" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1191"></td>
        <td id="LC1191" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For these tasks, some linguistic phenomena are particularly important,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1192" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1192"></td>
        <td id="LC1192" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">such as negation and hedging</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1193" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1193"></td>
        <td id="LC1193" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(including adverbs like <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{possibly}, modals like <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{may}, and verbs of speculation like <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{suggest}).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1194" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1194"></td>
        <td id="LC1194" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">When it comes to identifying facts asserted in a document,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1195" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1195"></td>
        <td id="LC1195" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">a clause that has been negated or hedged should be treated with caution.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1196" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1196"></td>
        <td id="LC1196" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{mackinlay2012biomed} consider the biomedical domain,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1197" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1197"></td>
        <td id="LC1197" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">evaluating on the BioNLP 2009 Shared Task <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{kim2009task},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1198" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1198"></td>
        <td id="LC1198" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where they outperform previous approaches for negation, but not for speculation.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1199" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1199"></td>
        <td id="LC1199" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{velldal2012specneg} consider negation and speculation in biomedical text,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1200" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1200"></td>
        <td id="LC1200" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">evaluating on the CoNLL 2010 Shared Task <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{farkas2010task},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1201" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1201"></td>
        <td id="LC1201" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where they outperform previous approaches.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1202" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1202"></td>
        <td id="LC1202" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{packard2014neg} propose a general-purpose method for finding the scope of negation in an MRS,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1203" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1203"></td>
        <td id="LC1203" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">evaluating on the *SEM 2012 Shared Task <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{morante2012task}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1204" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1204"></td>
        <td id="LC1204" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">They find that converting the output of the ERG with a relatively simple set of rules</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1205" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1205"></td>
        <td id="LC1205" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">achieves high performance on this dataset,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1206" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1206"></td>
        <td id="LC1206" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and combining this approach with a purely statistical system</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1207" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1207"></td>
        <td id="LC1207" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">outperforms previous approaches.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1208" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1208"></td>
        <td id="LC1208" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{zamaraeva2018pathology} use the ERG for negation detection and then</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1209" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1209"></td>
        <td id="LC1209" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">use that inforamtion to refine the (machine-learning) features in a </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1210" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1210"></td>
        <td id="LC1210" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">system that classifies pathology reports and improve system performance.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1211" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1211"></td>
        <td id="LC1211" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A common finding from these studies</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1212" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1212"></td>
        <td id="LC1212" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">is that a system using the output of the ERG</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1213" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1213"></td>
        <td id="LC1213" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">tends to have high precision (items identified by the system tend to be correct)</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1214" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1214"></td>
        <td id="LC1214" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">but low recall (items are often overlooked by the system).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1215" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1215"></td>
        <td id="LC1215" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">One reason for low recall is that the grammar does not cover all sentences in natural text.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1216" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1216"></td>
        <td id="LC1216" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">As we will see in Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:downstream:data},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1217" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1217"></td>
        <td id="LC1217" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">recent work on robust parsing may help to close this coverage gap.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1218" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1218"></td>
        <td id="LC1218" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1219" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1219"></td>
        <td id="LC1219" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Negation resolution is also included in <span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{oepen2017extrinsic}&#39;s</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1220" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1220"></td>
        <td id="LC1220" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Shared Task on Extrinsic Parser Evaluation.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1221" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1221"></td>
        <td id="LC1221" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">As mentioned in Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:prac:dep},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1222" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1222"></td>
        <td id="LC1222" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">dependency graphs can provide a useful tool in NLP tasks,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1223" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1223"></td>
        <td id="LC1223" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and this shared task aims to evaluate the use of dependency representations (both semantic and syntactic),</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1224" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1224"></td>
        <td id="LC1224" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">for three downstream applications:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1225" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1225"></td>
        <td id="LC1225" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">biomedical information extraction, negation resolution, and fine-grained opinion analysis.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1226" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1226"></td>
        <td id="LC1226" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Some participating teams use DM dependencies <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{schuster2017dep,chen2017dep}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1227" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1227"></td>
        <td id="LC1227" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The results of this shared task suggest that,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1228" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1228"></td>
        <td id="LC1228" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">compared to other dependency representations,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1229" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1229"></td>
        <td id="LC1229" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">DM is particularly useful for negation resolution.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1230" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1230"></td>
        <td id="LC1230" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1231" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1231"></td>
        <td id="LC1231" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Another task where dependency graphs have been used is <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{summarization}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1232" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1232"></td>
        <td id="LC1232" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Most existing work on this task focuses on so-called <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{extractive summarization}:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1233" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1233"></td>
        <td id="LC1233" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">given an input document, a system forms a summary by extracting short sections of the input.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1234" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1234"></td>
        <td id="LC1234" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">This is in contrast to <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{abstractive summarization},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1235" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1235"></td>
        <td id="LC1235" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where a system generates new text based on the input document.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1236" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1236"></td>
        <td id="LC1236" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Extractive summarization is limited, but widely used because it is easier to implement.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1237" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1237"></td>
        <td id="LC1237" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{fang2016summarise} show how a wide-coverage grammar like the ERG</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1238" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1238"></td>
        <td id="LC1238" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">makes it possible to implement an abstractive summarizer with state-of-the-art performance.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1239" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1239"></td>
        <td id="LC1239" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">After parsing the input document into logical propositions,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1240" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1240"></td>
        <td id="LC1240" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the summarizer prunes the set of propositions using a cognitively inspired model.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1241" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1241"></td>
        <td id="LC1241" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A summary is then generated based on the pruned set of propositions.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1242" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1242"></td>
        <td id="LC1242" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Because no text is directly extracted from the input document,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1243" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1243"></td>
        <td id="LC1243" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">it is possible to a generate a more concise summary.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1244" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1244"></td>
        <td id="LC1244" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1245" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1245"></td>
        <td id="LC1245" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Finally, no discussion of NLP tasks would be complete without including <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{machine translation}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1246" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1246"></td>
        <td id="LC1246" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A traditional grammar-based approach uses three grammars:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1247" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1247"></td>
        <td id="LC1247" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">a grammar for the source language,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1248" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1248"></td>
        <td id="LC1248" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">a grammar for the target language,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1249" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1249"></td>
        <td id="LC1249" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and a <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{transfer grammar}, which converts semantic representations for the source language</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1250" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1250"></td>
        <td id="LC1250" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">to semantic representations for the target language <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{OVL2007a-u,bond2011deep}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1251" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1251"></td>
        <td id="LC1251" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Translation proceeds in three steps:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1252" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1252"></td>
        <td id="LC1252" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">parse the source sentence, transfer the semantic representation, and generate a target sentence.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1253" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1253"></td>
        <td id="LC1253" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The transfer grammar is needed both to find appropriate lexical items,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1254" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1254"></td>
        <td id="LC1254" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and also to convert semantic representations</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1255" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1255"></td>
        <td id="LC1255" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">when languages differ in how an idea might be expressed.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1256" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1256"></td>
        <td id="LC1256" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The difficulty in writing a transfer grammar</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1257" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1257"></td>
        <td id="LC1257" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">that is robust enough to deal with arbitrary input text</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1258" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1258"></td>
        <td id="LC1258" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">means that statistical systems might be preferred.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1259" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1259"></td>
        <td id="LC1259" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{horvat2017translate} explores the use of statistical techniques,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1260" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1260"></td>
        <td id="LC1260" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">skipping out the transfer stage:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1261" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1261"></td>
        <td id="LC1261" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">a target-language sentence is generated directly</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1262" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1262"></td>
        <td id="LC1262" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">from a semantic representation for the source language.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1263" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1263"></td>
        <td id="LC1263" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{goodman2018translate} explores the use of statistical techniques</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1264" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1264"></td>
        <td id="LC1264" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">within the paradigm of parsing, transferring, and generating.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1265" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1265"></td>
        <td id="LC1265" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>TODO expand?</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1266" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1266"></td>
        <td id="LC1266" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1267" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1267"></td>
        <td id="LC1267" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>TODO check:</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1268" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1268"></td>
        <td id="LC1268" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> http://www.let.rug.nl/vannoord/papers/</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1269" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1269"></td>
        <td id="LC1269" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> http://heartofgold.dfki.de/Publications_Applications.html</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1270" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1270"></td>
        <td id="LC1270" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> http://www.nactem.ac.uk/enju/</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1271" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1271"></td>
        <td id="LC1271" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1272" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1272"></td>
        <td id="LC1272" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1273" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1273"></td>
        <td id="LC1273" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1274" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1274"></td>
        <td id="LC1274" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsubsection</span>{Data for machine learning}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1275" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1275"></td>
        <td id="LC1275" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{cl:downstream:data}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1276" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1276"></td>
        <td id="LC1276" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1277" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1277"></td>
        <td id="LC1277" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:downstream:nlp},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1278" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1278"></td>
        <td id="LC1278" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">we described how HPSG grammars can be directly incorporated into NLP systems.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1279" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1279"></td>
        <td id="LC1279" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Another use of HPSG grammars in NLP</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1280" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1280"></td>
        <td id="LC1280" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">is to generate data, on which a statistical system can be trained.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1281" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1281"></td>
        <td id="LC1281" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1282" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1282"></td>
        <td id="LC1282" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For example, one limitation of using an HPSG grammar in an NLP system</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1283" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1283"></td>
        <td id="LC1283" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">is that the grammar is unlikely to cover all sentences in the data <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{flickinger2012deepbank}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1284" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1284"></td>
        <td id="LC1284" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">One way to overcome this coverage gap</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1285" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1285"></td>
        <td id="LC1285" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">is to train a statistical system to produce the same output as the grammar.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1286" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1286"></td>
        <td id="LC1286" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The idea is that the trained system will be able to generalise to sentences that the grammar does not cover.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1287" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1287"></td>
        <td id="LC1287" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{oepen2014semeval} and <span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{oepen2015semeval}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1288" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1288"></td>
        <td id="LC1288" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">present shared tasks on semantic dependency parsing,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1289" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1289"></td>
        <td id="LC1289" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">including both DM dependencies and Enju predicate-argument structures.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1290" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1290"></td>
        <td id="LC1290" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The best-performing systems in these shared tasks</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1291" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1291"></td>
        <td id="LC1291" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">can produce dependency graphs almost as accurately as grammar-based parsers</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1292" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1292"></td>
        <td id="LC1292" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(for sentences where the grammar has coverage).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1293" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1293"></td>
        <td id="LC1293" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Similarly, <span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{buys2017parse} develop a parser for EDS and DMRS</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1294" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1294"></td>
        <td id="LC1294" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">which performs almost as well as a grammar-based parser,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1295" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1295"></td>
        <td id="LC1295" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">but has full coverage, and can run 70 times faster.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1296" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1296"></td>
        <td id="LC1296" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1297" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1297"></td>
        <td id="LC1297" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In fact, in more recent work, the difference in performance has been effectively closed.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1298" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1298"></td>
        <td id="LC1298" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{chen2018parse} consider parsing to EDS and DMRS graphs,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1299" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1299"></td>
        <td id="LC1299" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and actually achieve slightly higher accuracy with their system,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1300" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1300"></td>
        <td id="LC1300" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">compared to a grammar-based parser.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1301" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1301"></td>
        <td id="LC1301" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Unlike the previous statistical approaches,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1302" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1302"></td>
        <td id="LC1302" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citeauthor</span>{chen2018parse} do not just train on the desired dependency graphs,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1303" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1303"></td>
        <td id="LC1303" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">but also use information in the derivation tree.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1304" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1304"></td>
        <td id="LC1304" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">They suggest that using this information allows their system</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1305" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1305"></td>
        <td id="LC1305" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">to learn compositional rules mirroring composition in the grammar,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1306" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1306"></td>
        <td id="LC1306" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and thereby allows their system to generalise better.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1307" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1307"></td>
        <td id="LC1307" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>TODO numbers in the above paragraphs?</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1308" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1308"></td>
        <td id="LC1308" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1309" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1309"></td>
        <td id="LC1309" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Another application of HPSG-derived dependency graphs</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1310" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1310"></td>
        <td id="LC1310" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">is for <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{distributional semantics}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1311" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1311"></td>
        <td id="LC1311" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Here, the aim is to learn the meanings of words from a corpus,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1312" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1312"></td>
        <td id="LC1312" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">exploiting the fact that the context of a word tells us something about its meaning.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1313" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1313"></td>
        <td id="LC1313" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">This is known as the <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{distributional hypothesis},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1314" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1314"></td>
        <td id="LC1314" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">an idea with roots in American structuralism <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{harris1954distribution}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1315" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1315"></td>
        <td id="LC1315" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and British lexicology <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{firth1951collocation,firth1957company}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1316" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1316"></td>
        <td id="LC1316" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Most work on distributional semantics learns a <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{vector space model},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1317" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1317"></td>
        <td id="LC1317" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where the meaning of each word is represented as a point in a high-dimensional vector space</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1318" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1318"></td>
        <td id="LC1318" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(for an overview, see <span class="pl-c1">\citealt</span>{erk2012vector} and <span class="pl-c1">\citealt</span>{clark2015vector}).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1319" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1319"></td>
        <td id="LC1319" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">However, <span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{emerson2018functional} argues that</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1320" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1320"></td>
        <td id="LC1320" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">vector space models cannot capture various aspects of meaning,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1321" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1321"></td>
        <td id="LC1321" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">including logical structure, as well as phenomena like polysemy.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1322" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1322"></td>
        <td id="LC1322" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Instead, <span class="pl-c1">\citeauthor</span>{emerson2018functional} presents a distributional model</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1323" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1323"></td>
        <td id="LC1323" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">which can learn truth-conditional semantics,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1324" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1324"></td>
        <td id="LC1324" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">using a parsed corpus like WikiWoods (see Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:lang-doc:treebanks}).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1325" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1325"></td>
        <td id="LC1325" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">This approach relies on the semantic analyses given by a grammar,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1326" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1326"></td>
        <td id="LC1326" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">as well as the infrastructure to parse a large amount of text.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1327" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1327"></td>
        <td id="LC1327" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1328" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1328"></td>
        <td id="LC1328" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Finally, there are also applications using grammars not to parse, but to generate.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1329" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1329"></td>
        <td id="LC1329" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{kuhnle2018shapeworld} consider the task of <span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{visual question answering},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1330" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1330"></td>
        <td id="LC1330" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where a system is presented with an image and a question about the image,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1331" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1331"></td>
        <td id="LC1331" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and must answer the question.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1332" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1332"></td>
        <td id="LC1332" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">This task requires language understanding, reference resolution, and grounded reasoning,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1333" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1333"></td>
        <td id="LC1333" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">in a way that is relatively well-defined.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1334" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1334"></td>
        <td id="LC1334" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">However, for many existing datasets, there are biases in the questions</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1335" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1335"></td>
        <td id="LC1335" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">which mean that high performance can be achieved without true language understanding.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1336" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1336"></td>
        <td id="LC1336" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>TODO references</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1337" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1337"></td>
        <td id="LC1337" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For this reason, there is increasing interest in artificial datasets,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1338" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1338"></td>
        <td id="LC1338" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">which are controlled to make sure that high performance requires true understanding.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1339" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1339"></td>
        <td id="LC1339" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citeauthor</span>{kuhnle2018shapeworld} present ShapeWorld,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1340" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1340"></td>
        <td id="LC1340" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">a configurable system for generating artificial data.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1341" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1341"></td>
        <td id="LC1341" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The system generates an abstract representation of a scene</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1342" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1342"></td>
        <td id="LC1342" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(coloured shapes in different configurations),</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1343" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1343"></td>
        <td id="LC1343" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and then generates an image and a caption based on this representation.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1344" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1344"></td>
        <td id="LC1344" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The use of a broad-coverage grammar is crucial</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1345" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1345"></td>
        <td id="LC1345" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">in allowing the system to be configurable</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1346" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1346"></td>
        <td id="LC1346" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and scale across a variety of syntactic constructions.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1347" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1347"></td>
        <td id="LC1347" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1348" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1348"></td>
        <td id="LC1348" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1349" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1349"></td>
        <td id="LC1349" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1350" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1350"></td>
        <td id="LC1350" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\section</span>{Linguistic Insights}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1351" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1351"></td>
        <td id="LC1351" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{cl:insight}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1352" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1352"></td>
        <td id="LC1352" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1353" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1353"></td>
        <td id="LC1353" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:lang-doc} above, we described multiple ways in which computational methods can be used in the service of linguistic research, especially in testing linguistic hypotheses. Here, we highlight a few ways in which grammar eningineering work in HPSG has turned up linguistic insights that had not previously been discovered through non-computational means.<span class="pl-c1">\footnote</span>{For similar reflections from the point of view of LFG, see <span class="pl-c1">\citealt</span>{King:16}}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1354" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1354"></td>
        <td id="LC1354" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1355" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1355"></td>
        <td id="LC1355" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsection</span>{Ambiguity} <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>Guy</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1356" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1356"></td>
        <td id="LC1356" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1357" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1357"></td>
        <td id="LC1357" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">As discussed in Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:prac:rank},</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1358" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1358"></td>
        <td id="LC1358" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the scale of ambiguity has become clear now that broad-coverage precision grammars are available.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1359" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1359"></td>
        <td id="LC1359" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">By taking both coverage and precision seriously,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1360" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1360"></td>
        <td id="LC1360" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">it is possible to investigate ambiguity on a large scale,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1361" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1361"></td>
        <td id="LC1361" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">quantifying the sources of ambiguity and the information needed to resolve it.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1362" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1362"></td>
        <td id="LC1362" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For example, <span class="pl-c1">\citet</span>{Tou:Man:Shi:Fli:Oep:02,Tou:Man:Fli:Oep:05}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1363" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1363"></td>
        <td id="LC1363" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">found that in the Redwoods treebank (3rd Growth),</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1364" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1364"></td>
        <td id="LC1364" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">roughly half of the ambiguity was lexical, and half syntactic.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1365" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1365"></td>
        <td id="LC1365" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> Baseline accuracy: .227 ~ choosing out of 4.41 parses</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1366" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1366"></td>
        <td id="LC1366" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> Accuracy given lexical tags: .488 ~ choosing out of 2.05 parses, roughly square root of above</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1367" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1367"></td>
        <td id="LC1367" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">They also showed how combining sources of information</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1368" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1368"></td>
        <td id="LC1368" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(such as both semantic and syntactic information)</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1369" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1369"></td>
        <td id="LC1369" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">is important for resolving ambiguity,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1370" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1370"></td>
        <td id="LC1370" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">consistent with probabilistic approaches in psycholinguistics.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1371" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1371"></td>
        <td id="LC1371" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1372" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1372"></td>
        <td id="LC1372" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1373" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1373"></td>
        <td id="LC1373" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsection</span>{Long-tail phenomena} <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> Emily</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1374" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1374"></td>
        <td id="LC1374" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">One of the strengths of HPSG as a theoretical framework is that it allows for the analysis of both `core&#39; and `peripheral&#39; phenomena within a single, integrated model. When working with actual data and large scale gramamrs, it quickly becomes apparent just how long the long-tail of `peripheral&#39; phenomena is. Furthermore, the sustained development of broad-coverage linguistic resources makes it possible to bring more and more low-frequency phenomena or low-frequency variations on relatively high-frequency phenomena into view. A case in point is the range of raising and control valence frames found in the ERG \cite{Flickinger2000a,Flickinger2011a-u}. As of the 2018 release, the ERG includes over 60 types for raising and control predicates, including verbs, adjectives, and nouns, many of which are not otherwise discussed in the syntactic literature. These include such low-frequency types as the one for \textit{incumbent} which requires an explitive \textit{it} subject, an obligatory \textit{(up)on} PP subject, and an infinitival VP complement and establishes a control relation between the object of \textit{on} and the VP&#39;s missing subject:\footnote{Our thanks to Dan Flickinger for this example.}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1375" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1375"></td>
        <td id="LC1375" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1376" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1376"></td>
        <td id="LC1376" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{exe}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1377" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1377"></td>
        <td id="LC1377" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\ex\label</span>{cl:incumbent} </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1378" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1378"></td>
        <td id="LC1378" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">It is incumbent on you to speak plainly.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1379" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1379"></td>
        <td id="LC1379" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{exe}</td>

        <td id="L1391" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1391"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L1392" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1392"></td>
        <td id="LC1392" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> i.e. a predicate for each content word, rather than using semantic primitives</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1393" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1393"></td>
        <td id="LC1393" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> EMB 2019-02-21 That makes sense, but I don&#39;t have the energy for it right</span></td>

        <td id="LC1394" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> now, so commenting this out for now.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1395" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1395"></td>
        <td id="LC1395" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1396" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1396"></td>
        <td id="LC1396" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsection</span>{Analysis-order effects}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1397" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1397"></td>
        <td id="LC1397" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Grammar engineering means making analyses</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1398" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1398"></td>
        <td id="LC1398" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">specific and then being able to build on them. This has both benefits</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1399" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1399"></td>
        <td id="LC1399" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and drawbacks: One the one hand, it means that additional grammar</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1400" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1400"></td>
        <td id="LC1400" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">engineering work can build directly on the results of previous</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1401" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1401"></td>
        <td id="LC1401" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">work. It also means that any additional grammar engineering work is</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1402" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1402"></td>
        <td id="LC1402" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">constrained by the work it is building on.  <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{Fokkens:14} observes</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1403" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1403"></td>
        <td id="LC1403" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">this phenomenon and notes that it introduces artifacts: the form an</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1404" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1404"></td>
        <td id="LC1404" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">implemented grammar takes is partially the result of the order in</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1405" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1405"></td>
        <td id="LC1405" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">which the grammar engineer considered phenomena to implement. This is</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1406" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1406"></td>
        <td id="LC1406" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">probably also true for non-computational work, as theoretical ideas</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1407" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1407"></td>
        <td id="LC1407" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">developed with particular phenomena (and indeed languages) in mind</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1408" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1408"></td>
        <td id="LC1408" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">influence the questions with which researchers approach additional</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1409" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1409"></td>
        <td id="LC1409" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">phenomena. <span class="pl-c1">\citeauthor</span>{Fokkens:14} proposes that the methodology of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1410" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1410"></td>
        <td id="LC1410" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">meta-grammar engineering can be used to address this problem: Using</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1411" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1411"></td>
        <td id="LC1411" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">her CLIMB methodology, rather than deciding between analyses of a</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1412" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1412"></td>
        <td id="LC1412" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">given phenomenon without input from later-studied phenomena, the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1413" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1413"></td>
        <td id="LC1413" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">grammar engineer can maintain multiple competing analyses through time</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1414" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1414"></td>
        <td id="LC1414" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and break free, at least partially, of the effects of the timeline of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1415" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1415"></td>
        <td id="LC1415" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">grammar development. The central idea is that the grammar writer develops</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1416" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1416"></td>
        <td id="LC1416" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">a meta-grammar, like the Grammar Matrix customization system (see Section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{cl:lang-doc:gmcs}),</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1417" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1417"></td>
        <td id="LC1417" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">but for a single language. This customization system maintains</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1418" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1418"></td>
        <td id="LC1418" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">alternate analyses of particular phenomena which are invoked via grammar</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1419" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1419"></td>
        <td id="LC1419" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">specifications so the different versions of the grammar can be compiled</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1420" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1420"></td>
        <td id="LC1420" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and tested.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1421" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1421"></td>
        <td id="LC1421" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1422" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1422"></td>
        <td id="LC1422" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1423" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1423"></td>
        <td id="LC1423" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\section</span>{Summary}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1424" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1424"></td>
        <td id="LC1424" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1425" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1425"></td>
        <td id="LC1425" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In this chapter, we have attempted to illuminate the landscape of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1426" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1426"></td>
        <td id="LC1426" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">computational work in HPSG. We have discussed how HPSG as a theory</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1427" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1427"></td>
        <td id="LC1427" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">supports computational work, described large-scale computational</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1428" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1428"></td>
        <td id="LC1428" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">projects that use HPSG, highlighted some applications of implemented</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1429" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1429"></td>
        <td id="LC1429" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">grammars in HPSG, and explored ways in which computational work can</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1430" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1430"></td>
        <td id="LC1430" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">inform linguistic research. This field is very active and our overview</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1431" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1431"></td>
        <td id="LC1431" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">necessarily incomplete. Nonetheless, it is our hope that the pointers</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1432" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1432"></td>
        <td id="LC1432" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and overview provided in this chapter will serve to help interested readers</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1433" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1433"></td>
        <td id="LC1433" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">connect with on-going research in computational linguistics using HPSG.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1434" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1434"></td>
        <td id="LC1434" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1435" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1435"></td>
        <td id="LC1435" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> EMB 2019-02-21 Okay, that&#39;s kinda uninspired, but the ``summary&#39;&#39; is</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1436" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1436"></td>
